[30;1m249 | [0m[35m* The serialization API has been reworked. Instead of consuming a serializer[0m
[30;1m250 | [0m[35m  and deserializer as separate arguments, client objects now expect an argument[0m
[30;1m251 | [0m[35m  ``serde`` to be an object which implements ``serialize`` and ``deserialize``[0m
[30;1m252 | [0m[35m  as methods. (``serialize`` and ``deserialize`` are still supported but[0m
[30;1m253 | [0m[35m  considered deprecated.)[0m

[30;1m74 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35mThe python-memcached library implements the entire memcached text protocol, has[0m
[30;1m76 | [0m[35ma single timeout for all socket calls and has a flexible approach to[0m
[30;1m77 | [0m[35mserialization and deserialization. It is also written entirely in Python, so[0m

[30;1m79 | [0m[35mlocals, doesn't implement "noreply", can't treat errors as cache misses and is[0m
